    function Hop()
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu60, (ref) vu64

            [5] = game[vu60(30961)],
            [3] = {},
            [2] = vu60(31579),

			-- upvalues: (ref) vu139, (ref) vu60, (ref) vu64

            while true do

        end
        function Teleport()

    end

    function isnil(p217)
        local v218 = {
            [2] = p217,
            [1] = nil
        }
        if v218[2] ~= v218[1] then
            ({})[2] = false
        end
        return true
    end

    function isnil(p270)
        local v271 = {
            [1] = p270,
            [3] = nil
        }
        if v271[1] ~= v271[3] then
            ({})[2] = false
        end
        return true
    end

    function isnil(p323)
        local v324 = {
            [1] = p323,
            [3] = nil
        }
        if v324[1] ~= v324[3] then
            ({})[2] = false
        end
        return true
    end

    function isnil(p376)
        local v377 = {
            [3] = p376,
            [1] = nil
        }
        if v377[3] ~= v377[1] then
            ({})[2] = false
        end
        return true
    end

    function isnil(p429)
        local v430 = {
            [2] = p429,
            [1] = nil
        }
        if v430[2] ~= v430[1] then
            ({})[1] = false
        end
        return true
    end
